create table DG_Schema(
schema_ID int,
schema_name varchar(80),
description varchar(80),
create_date date,
modify_date date,
constraint DG_Schema_schema_ID_PK primary key (schema_ID));

insert into DG_Schema values(	1,'Zeota','Zeota','	8/17/2021	','		');
insert into DG_Schema values(	2,'SP','SP','	8/10/2021	','		');

create table DG_Tables(
Table_ID varchar(80),
Table_Name varchar(80),
Database_ID int,
description varchar(80),
create_date date,
modify_date date,
constraint DG_Tables_Table_ID_PK primary key (Table_ID),
CONSTRAINT DG_Tables_Database_ID_FK FOREIGN KEY (Database_ID) REFERENCES DG_Schema(schema_ID));

create table DG_Attributes(
Table_id varchar(80),
Table_Name varchar(80),
Attributes_ID varchar(80),
Attributes_Name	varchar(80),
comment	varchar(80),
create_date	date,
modify_date date,
constraint DG_Attributes_Attributes_ID_PK primary key (Attributes_ID),
CONSTRAINT DG_Attributes_Table_ID_FK FOREIGN KEY (Table_ID) REFERENCES DG_Tables(Table_ID));

create table DG_Attributes_PK(
Constraint_name varchar(80),
Constraint_Type varchar(80),
PK_ID	varchar(80),
Attributes_ID varchar(80),
Comment	varchar(80),
create_date date,
modify_date date,
constraint DG_Attributes_PK_PK_ID_Attributes_ID_PK primary key (PK_ID,Attributes_ID),

create table DG_Attributes_Index(
Constraint_name varchar(80),
Constraint_Type varchar(80),
IDX_ID	varchar(80),
Attributes_ID varchar(80),
Comment	varchar(80),
create_date	date,
modify_date date,
constraint DG_Attributes_Index_IDX_ID_Attributes_ID_PK primary key (IDX_ID,Attributes_ID),
CONSTRAINT DG_Attributes_Index_Attributes_ID_FK FOREIGN KEY (Attributes_ID) REFERENCES DG_Attributes(Attributes_ID));

create table DG_Attributes_FK(
Constraint_name varchar(80),
Constraint_Type varchar(80),
FK_ID	varchar(80),
Attributes_ID varchar(80),
Comment	varchar(80),
create_date	date,
modify_date date,
constraint DG_Attributes_FK_FK_ID_Attributes_ID_PK primary key (FK_ID,Attributes_ID),

create table DG_Attributes_NotNull(
Constraint_name varchar(80),
Constraint_Type varchar(80),
NN_ID	varchar(80),
Attributes_ID varchar(80),
Comment	varchar(80),
create_date	date,
modify_date date,
constraint DG_Attributes_NotNull_NN_ID_Attributes_ID_PK primary key (NN_ID,Attributes_ID),
CONSTRAINT DG_Attributes_NotNull_Attributes_ID_FK FOREIGN KEY (Attributes_ID) REFERENCES DG_Attributes(Attributes_ID));

create table DG_Attributes_ConstCheck(
Constraint_name varchar(80),
Constraint_Type varchar(80),
CC_ID	varchar(80),
Attributes_ID varchar(80),
Comment	varchar(80),
create_date	date,
modify_date date,
constraint DG_Attributes_ConstCheck_CC_ID_Attributes_ID_PK primary key (CC_ID,Attributes_ID),
CONSTRAINT DG_Attributes_ConstCheck_Attributes_ID_FK FOREIGN KEY (Attributes_ID) REFERENCES DG_Attributes(Attributes_ID));

create table DG_User_Unit_Role(	
User_ID varchar(80),
Role_ID varchar(80),
Unit_ID varchar(80),
definition	varchar(80),
start_date varchar(80),
end_date varchar(80),
create_date	date,
modify_date date,
constraint DG_User_Unit_Role_User_ID_Role_ID_Unit_ID_start_date_PK primary key (User_ID,Role_ID,Unit_ID,start_date),
CONSTRAINT DG_User_Unit_Role_User_ID_FK FOREIGN KEY (User_ID) REFERENCES DG_Users(User_ID),
CONSTRAINT DG_User_Unit_Role_Role_ID_FK FOREIGN KEY (Role_ID) REFERENCES DG_Role(Role_ID),
CONSTRAINT DG_User_Unit_Role_Unit_ID_FK FOREIGN KEY (Unit_ID) REFERENCES DG_Unit(Unit_ID));

URT_ID varchar(80),
Table_id varchar(80),
Role_ID	varchar(80),
Unit_ID varchar(80),
DB_Operation varchar(80),
definition varchar(80),
create_date	date,
modify_date date,
constraint DG_Unit_Role_Table_URT_ID_Table_id_Role_ID_Unit_ID_PK primary key (URT_ID,Table_id,Role_ID,Unit_ID,DB_Operation),
CONSTRAINT DG_Unit_Role_Table_Table_id_FK FOREIGN KEY (Table_id) REFERENCES DG_Tables(Table_id),
CONSTRAINT DG_Unit_Role_Table_Role_ID_FK FOREIGN KEY (Role_ID) REFERENCES DG_Role(Role_ID),
CONSTRAINT DG_Unit_Role_Table_Unit_ID_FK FOREIGN KEY (Unit_ID) REFERENCES DG_Unit(Unit_ID));

create table DG_Views(	
V_name varchar(80),
View_ID varchar(80),
description	varchar(80),
create_date	date,
modify_date date,
constraint DG_View_Table_ID_View_ID_PK primary key (View_ID));


create table DG_View_Table(	
Table_ID varchar(80),
View_ID varchar(80),
description	varchar(80),
definition	varchar(80),
create_date	date,
modify_date date,
constraint DG_View_Table_Table_ID_View_ID_PK primary key (Table_ID,View_ID),
CONSTRAINT DG_View_Table_Table_ID_FK FOREIGN KEY (Table_ID) REFERENCES DG_Tables(Table_ID),
CONSTRAINT DG_View_Table_View_ID_FK FOREIGN KEY (View_ID) REFERENCES DG_Views(View_ID));

create table DG_Base_Trigger_Table(	
Trigger_ID varchar(80),
Table_ID varchar(80),
description	varchar(80),
TName	varchar(80),
create_date	date,
modify_date date,
constraint DG_Base_Trigger_Table_Trigger_ID_Table_ID_PK primary key (Trigger_ID,Table_ID),
CONSTRAINT DG_Base_Trigger_Table_Table_ID_PK FOREIGN KEY (Table_ID) REFERENCES DG_Tables(Table_ID));

Table_ID varchar(80),

constraint DG_Audit_Table_Audit_ID_Table_ID_PK primary key (Audit_ID,Table_ID),
